üá∑üá∫ On August 22, Russia celebrates National Flag Day, established by Presidential Executive Order On National Flag Day of the Russian Federation dated August 20, 1994.

#OTD, we pay tribute to the official state symbol of Russia, which, along with its emblem and anthem, marks its sovereignty and independence, and reaffirms the continuity of many generations of the country‚Äôs multiethnic people.

‚öìÔ∏è The Russian tricolor is more than three centuries old. Peter the Great is considered the creator: in 1705, he issued an order according to which they should raise a white-blue-and-red flag ‚Äúon all merchant ships.‚Äù However, it was only given official national flag status in 1896, on the eve of the coronation of Nicholas II.

On December 25, 2000, the Federal Constitutional Law On the State Flag of the Russian Federation was adopted, under which the state flag of Russia was a rectangular panel of three equal horizontal stripes: the top one was white, the middle one was blue and the bottom one was red.

‚ö™Ô∏èüîµüî¥ It is believed that white represents peace and dignity; blue, loyalty and honesty; and red, courage and valour.

Today, the tricolor has firmly become part of our lives as an integral element of Russian statehood, a symbol of the unity of the people, their devotion to the Fatherland, and their readiness to defend Russia‚Äôs national interests.

Angel
‚ö°Ô∏èüá™üá¨üåç Egypt has become a new member of the BRICS organization, what does this mean?

First of all, to understand what joining BRICS means for Egypt, we have to understand why BRICS accepted the Egyptian request to join the organization in the first place.

The Russian Foreign Minister, Mr.Lavrov, stated that the standards and procedures to accept new members were based on many factors, including the prestige, political weight, and position on the international relations sphere, and everyone having "common ideas", which include those who support a multipolar world order, international relations becoming more fair and democratic, and the increase of the developing world and the global south in the mechanisms of the global world order.

I am not very educated in economics, but from what I know, Egyptian trade with BRICS countries reached 4.5 billion US dollars, Egypt and South Africa, alongside Nigeria and other North African countries, are considered the economic powerhouses of the continent.

Egypt is considered the main lynchpin of security and order in the Middle East and North Africa, the collapse of our neighbors to the south, east, and west, and the fact we are still standing, shows that the security services have done commendable services in carrying out their tasks.

Egypt is also a country that does not belong to a sole hegemonic bloc, Egypt is Egypt and Egypt wants Egyptian interests, Egypt opposes Russian influence in Libya and Sudan, but agrees with Russia on several cases like Wheat or Energy, Egypt opposes Chinese policies in the Middle East, but has an understanding with it in Africa.

Whether the Russians and the Chinese came to the conclusion that cooperation on several files outweigh the possible repercussions of being opposed on others, or they think they can turn us to their side fully, is unknown, but what is known for sure is that we are now linked together - for good or ill.

Egyptian economic development has been at least noted by international observes at times.

Egypt, in 7 years, built over 10,000 new factories, the industrial sectors value increased from 22 billion US dollars to over 60 billion US dollars, the GDP of Egypt from 2017 grew from 235 to 476 billion US dollars in 2022, the exports from 2014 to 2021 also doubled, growing from a value of 20 billion US dollars to 45.

Egyptian Roads were ranked 107th globally on 2017, in 2022, they were ranked 28th, and on Africa they were ranked the 2nd on the continent, over 7,000kms of roads were built in 8 years at a cost of around 200 billion US dollars, this reduced the rate of accidents and increased the efficiency of roads and transportation

The potential is there, we will just have to wait and see how it will be used.
